<SectionContent

  id="operation-get_schedules_v1_workflows_schedules_get_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.schedules.getSchedules();

  for await (const page of result) {
    console.log(page);
  }
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.schedules.get_schedules()

    while res is not None:
        # Handle items

        res = res.next()


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

</OperationTitleSection>

_Schedule Workflow_

Schedule Workflow

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-schedule_workflow_v1_workflows_schedules_post_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-schedule_workflow_v1_workflows_schedules_post_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.schedules.scheduleWorkflow({
    schedule: {
      input: "<value>",
    },
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-schedule_workflow_v1_workflows_schedules_post_code-samples_python"
  tags={{"codeSample":"python"}}
>

Python

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-schedule_workflow_v1_workflows_schedules_post_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.schedules.schedule_workflow(schedule={
        "input": "<value>",
    })

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-schedule_workflow_v1_workflows_schedules_post_code-samples_curl"
  tags={{"codeSample":"curl"}}
>

cURL

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-schedule_workflow_v1_workflows_schedules_post_code-samples_curl"
>

<CodeSample>

```curl
curl https://api.mistral.ai/v1/workflows/schedules \
 -X POST \
 -H 'Authorization: Bearer YOUR_APIKEY_HERE' \
 -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
 -d '{
  "schedule": {
    "input": "Example input."
  }
}'
```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

<ExpandablePropertyTitle slot="title">

##### schedule \{#operation-schedule_workflow_v1_workflows_schedules_post_request_schedule\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Specification of the times scheduled actions may occur.

The times are the union of :py:attr:`calendars`, :py:attr:`intervals`, and
:py:attr:`cron_expressions` excluding anything in :py:attr:`skip`.

Used for input where schedule_id is optional (can be provided or auto-generated).

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

and this value if present (but not past the next schedule).

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/workflows/schedules/\{schedule\_id\} \{#operation-get_schedule_v1_workflows_schedules_schedule_id_get\}

</OperationTitleSection>

<OperationSummarySection slot="summary">

_Get Schedule_

</OperationSummarySection>

<OperationDescriptionSection slot="description">

Get Schedule

</OperationDescriptionSection>

<OperationCodeSamplesSection slot="code-samples">

<CodeSampleTabbedSection>

<CodeSampleTab
  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_schedule_v1_workflows_schedules_schedule_id_get_code-samples_typescript"
  tags={{"codeSample":"typescript"}}
>

TypeScript

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_schedule_v1_workflows_schedules_schedule_id_get_code-samples_typescript"
>

<CodeSample>

```typescript
import { Mistral } from "@mistralai/mistralai";

const mistral = new Mistral({
  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",
});

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.schedules.getSchedule({
    scheduleId: "<id>",
  });

  console.log(result);
}

run();

```

</CodeSample>

</SectionContent>

  slot="tab"
  id="operation-get_schedule_v1_workflows_schedules_schedule_id_get_code-samples_python"

>

</CodeSampleTab>

<SectionContent
  slot="content"
  id="operation-get_schedule_v1_workflows_schedules_schedule_id_get_code-samples_python"
>

<CodeSample>

```python
from mistralai.client import Mistral
import os


with Mistral(
    api_key=os.getenv("MISTRAL_API_KEY", ""),
) as mistral:

    res = mistral.workflows.schedules.get_schedule(schedule_id="<id>")

    # Handle response
    print(res)


```

  apiKey: "MISTRAL_API_KEY",

async function run() {
  const result = await mistral.workflows.schedules.updateSchedule({
    scheduleId: "<id>",
    workflowScheduleUpdateRequest: {

    },
  });

##### schedule \{#operation-update_schedule_v1_workflows_schedules_schedule_id_patch_request_schedule\}

</ExpandablePropertyTitle>

<ExpandablePropertyDescription slot="description">

Schedule definition for partial updates.

All fields are optional (inherited from _ScheduleRequestBase). Only explicitly-set
fields are applied during an update; unset fields preserve the existing schedule values.

</ExpandablePropertyDescription>
